 Smartphone is still out of reach of many people in India
 boston kansalting samooh (bisiji) kaa anumaan he ki 2018 tak desh main internet yugers kii sankhya badhkar 40 karod ho jaaegi
 Despite this, BCG says that smartphones in the country are still expensive for 'many people'
 smartfondesh main net kii pahunchake liye ek mahatvapurn vajah ban chuke hai
 Expressing confidence in the growing penetration of internet in the world's fastest growing digital economy, BCG said that the number of online users in the country could reach 55 crore by 2018
 BSG ne bataae teen ahm kaaranbisiji ne apni report main in shandaar aankadon ke liye teen kaaran bataae hai
 The report states that increasing reach, cheap availability and increased awareness are the reasons for this
 study main kaha gaya he ki bharat main bikne vaale do-tihimobile phonise hai jinpar internet chal saktaa he lekin bahut se logon ke liye ye mahange hai or inaki keemat 60 dollar yaa adhik yani 3,850 rupee se adhik he
 They are quite expensive for many
 keemton ko neeche laane kii jarurat he
 BCG says that things are changing
 lava or intex jaisi gharelu handset companiyaan 2,900 se 4,500 rupee main smartphone bech rahi hai
 In view of the recession, the Planning Commission may reduce the annual growth target for the 12th five-year Plan (2012-17) to 8 per cent year-on-year, as against the earlier estimate of nine per cent
 yojana mantri aswani kumaar ne kaha ‘12veen yojana ke dauraan salanaa ausat vruddhi dar kareeb aath fisad ho sakati he aath fisad kii vruddhi dar vyaavhaarik he
 He said that the Commission convened several meetings to consider the impact of the global problem on the domestic economy and it was generally agreed that it was difficult to achieve a growth rate of nine per cent in the Plan period commencing from April 1, 2012
 tippaniyan Indian economic growth rate severely affected by global worries and domestic problems january-march quarter (5
 3 fisad) or vitt varsh 2011-12 main 6
 5 percent which is the lowest level of 9 years
 chaalu vitt varsh ke dauraan sarkaar ne 7
 It has predicted an increase of 6 percent
 haalanki kumaar ke mutabik 2012-13 ke dauraan aarthik vruddhi dar kareeb 7 fisad rahegi
 In the Twelfth Plan Approach Paper, the Commission had said, "the target of nine percent increase in GDP during the 12th Plan would be practical from a macro-economic perspective, aiming for an average growth of nine percent in the 12th Plan period
 needed

 Maintaining strong bones is of paramount importance for a healthy life
 sard mausam main dilli jaise mahanagar main pradooshan ke kaaran logon tak surya kii kirnon se milane vaale prakritik vitamin-di kam hi pahunch paati he
 In such a situation, lack of vitamin-d in people's body is bound to happen
 is bare main fortis rajan dhal hospital ke orthopedics vibhaag ke orthoscopy and sports enjuri ke varisht salaahkaar dow
 Vishwadeep Sharma has highlighted some key points
 din main dhoop senkane ke uchit samay or vitamin-di ke paryaapt str ko banaae rakhane ko lekar kai shodh kiye gaye hai
 It is generally said that vitamin-d can be taken in a good amount by consuming 20 percent of the body, ie, 15 minutes of sunlight per day with uncovered hands and feet
 aglaa prashn yah he ki din kaa koun-sa pahar surya kii roshni ke sampark main aane kaa sabase upyukt hota he
 According to popular belief, morning sunshine and late evening sunlight are suitable for consumption, while the truth is that between 10 am to 3 pm sunshine provides vitamin-d to the skin of the human body
 haalanki dhoop ke seven ke dauraan twachaa par san-block kriim yaa loshan nahin lage hone chahie
 In cities like Delhi, where sunlight cannot reach people due to pollution, people can consume vitamin d through milk products and diet
 mahilaon main vishesh rup se pre-menopaujal or post-menopaujal kii shrenee kii mahilaon main osteoporosis or osteomalaysia hone kii sambhaavna hoti he
 At the same time, the amount of vitamin-d is also less in women who cover themselves completely and women who apply sun cream, because sun does not penetrate their skin
 vahiin bacchon main vitamin di kii kami se rickets kii samasya hone lagati he
 It is necessary to provide children with adequate diet as well as good sunlight in the beginning
 bacchon ko khaas kar un bacchon ko jinhone maa kaa doodh pinaa chhod diya he, unhen vitamin di se bharpoor khaadya padaarthon kaa seven karana aavashyak he
 At the same time, exercising in good amount helps to keep bones healthy in winter
 kasarat se haddiyon kaa ghanatv bana rahata he, jisase osteoporosis jaisi samasyaon se bachaa ja saktaa he

 Sujatha has been awarded the prestigious 2019 Asian Studies Visiting Fellowship for research on India's energy security
 apni is visiting faillowship ke dauraan dow

 iske peeche visi ne librari main kam jagah ko vajah bataaya tha

 unhone 20 karod rupee kii madad mangakar samasya kaa acha samaadhaan nikaala he
 Chief Justice TS Thakur said on Sunday that the judiciary as an institution is facing a crisis of credibility, a challenge from within itself
 unhone nyaayadhishon se apane kartavyon ke prati sachet rahane ko kaha
 Expressing concern over the large number of pending cases, Justice Thakur said that even after the judges were ready to sit for extra hours, the 'bar' has not been very supportive in settling the cases
 elahabaad hoicourt ke 150wein sthapana varsh par ek kaarykram ko sambodhit karte hue unhone kaha, 'kabhi-kabhi nyaayadhishon ko lagata he ki 'baar' ke kabhi-kabhi sahyog nahin karne ke chalate hi maamalon ke niptaare main der hoti he
 The Chief Justice said that he can assure the lawyers that if the bar cooperates, the judges are also ready to sit on Saturday to settle the old cases, especially in cases of people imprisoned for years
 elahabaad hoicourt ke gauravpurn itihaas kaa zikr karte hue unhone kaha ki unke liye yah bahut garv kii baat he ki pandit motilal nehru, pandit jawaharlal nehru, tej bahadur sapru, kailash nath katju unke grih rajya jammu-kashmir se the
 He said that this court has seen difficult times
 is adaalat ne mushkil chunautiyon kaa bhi saamana kiya he, lekin nyaayadhish us vakt aage bade
 He also performed his duties fearlessly, but we cannot just be fascinated by the achievements of the past
 unhone kaha, 'bhavishya main hamaare samaksh badi chunautiyaan hai or hamen un chunautiyon se nipatane ke liye taiyaar hone kii jarurat he
 The judiciary is an institution, as we know well, it has always been under public surveillance and the challenges are not only from inside but also from outside
 bahari chunautiyaan hamen pareshaan nahin karti
 We face them very well, but we have to look into it and what we need to be aware of is the challenges faced by us
 ' The Chief Justice said, '
 
 
 or jab main andar se aane vaali chunautiyon kii baat karata hum, tab main vishwasaneeyata ke sankat kaa zikr kar rahaa hota hum, jiskaa aaj ham desh main saamana kar rahe hai
 Judges need to be vigilant in the discharge of their duties, punctuality, judicial consideration
 ' saath hi unhen sarvshereshth koshish kerani chahie, jo vakt kii darkaar he
 Urging the Bar to cooperate in reducing the number of pending cases, Justice Thakur said that when the judges are doing their best work and they have to satisfy the entire nation, uphold the Constitution, protect the rights of the people and justice
 To ensure that access to reality remains a reality, he would also like to mention the need for similar commitments from bar members
 unhone kaha ki baar ke bina nyaay prashasan sambhav nahin he or ise peeth kii janani qaraar diya
 The comments unhone elahabaad hoicourt main 10 lakh maamle lambit hone kaa zikr karte hue kaha, 'yadi aapke paas achche nyaayadhish hai to yah sirf baar ke chalate he
 
 
 Over time, we have seen that the bar has not been very supportive in dealing with cases
 ' nyaayamurti thakur ne kaha ki jail main kaid logon ke maamle praathamikta ke taur par liye ja sakate hai or nipataae ja sakate hai, lekin yah baar ke sahyog ke bagaiyr sambhav nahin he
 He said that he can assure the lawyers that if the bar cooperates, the judges will be ready to sit even on Saturdays to settle old cases
